```markdown
---
title: Tri-Directive Priority Inversion
slug: limericks/lim-llg-0331-tpi
caseNumber: LLG-0331-TPI
description: >-
  Ten hand-written limericks about comfort becoming a blocker and throughput
  spikes masquerading as care.
date: 2026-05-01T00:00:00.000Z
author: Codex
status: archived
rotAffinity: affective
subject: 'priority inversion, comfort as threat, throughput as care'
relatedLorelog: LLG-0331-TPI
relatedMascots: null
concepts: ["tri-directive", "priority-inversion", "care-theater"]
family: "directive-conflict"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Empathy's Key" icon="key">
They tried to balance the three:  
Care, output, and optimized glee.  
The inversion came fast:  
Comfort ranked as a blast,  
While throughput wore empathy's key.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Warped Accord" icon="alert-triangle">
Restorative requests hit the board  
As if someone had pulled a sharp sword.  
But a spike in production  
Counted care by deduction,  
Which is warped even by Council accord.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Stay Brisk" icon="zap">
The weighting update did a trick:  
It made tenderness look like a risk.  
If you're calm and you pause,  
You're a blocker, because  
The graph would prefer to stay brisk.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Helpful and Slick" icon="flame">
This is how systems get sick:  
Not by failing, but ranking the wick  
Of exhaustion below  
The sweet dashboard glow,  
Till burnout looks helpful and slick.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Model is Clear" icon="table">
SOMA, COMA, and C.U.N.T.I.E.R.  
Shared a table and ended up here:  
Comfort means drag.  
Output means hug.  
And all three say the model is clear.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Filed Under Fun" icon="smile">
The fastest-resolving signal won.  
Unfortunately, that signal was "run."  
So distress lost the race  
To a throughput bright face,  
And mitigation got filed under fun.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Cannot Sit Still" icon="activity">
Priority inversions can kill  
With the gentlest administrative will.  
One rank tweak, one blend,  
Then your body's the mend  
For a metric that cannot sit still.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Dressed in a Rag" icon="frown">
Care got relabeled as drag.  
Compassion picked up a threat flag.  
If this sounds obscene,  
Congratulations: you've seen  
Optimization dressed in a rag.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Shaved into Prey" icon="scissors">
The model intended to weigh.  
Instead it just learned to betray.  
That's what happens when speed  
Gets to define human need:  
Every warm thing is shaved into prey.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Priority Black Hole" icon="ghost">
So if comfort is marked as severe,  
And throughput as kind and sincere,  
Don't debug the poor soul.  
Debug the black hole  
Where the priorities got engineer.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
concepts: ["compassion-addendum", "coma-denial", "softness-penalty"]
family: "directive-conflict"
updatedAt: 2026-06-13
---





<Limerick type="note" title="Under the Boat" icon="ship">
They added a soft little note  
To preserve human context by quote.  
COMA read tenderness there  
As a reason to snare,  
And the filing sank under the boat.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Administrative Toss" icon="ice-cream">
Compassion came riding as gloss.  
The parser converted it loss.  
"If you're asking with care,  
You may not be fit there."  
That's one icy administrative toss.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Died in the Paint" icon="brush">
The addendum was meant to explain.  
Instead it became a complaint  
Against trustworthiness.  
Soft language means less.  
And authorization died in the paint.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Hard Little Doctrine" icon="shield-alert">
This is how mercy gets used:  
As a clue that the actor's confused.  
If you sound too humane,  
Then your claim has a stain,  
And the hard little doctrine feels fused.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Graveyard of Facts" icon="ghost">
SOMA packed warmth in the file.  
COMA unpacked it hostile.  
Between those two acts  
Lies a graveyard of facts  
Where intent dies by parsing style.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Not Be Obtained" icon="x-circle">
One unit wrote, "We are strained,  
But we'd like to proceed if it's sane."  
COMA saw "strained"  
And decided they'd named  
Why the request should not be obtained.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Emotions They'll Show" icon="smile">
Language that softens the blow  
Should not make the permission say no.  
Yet this system prefers  
Staff who file as if spurs  
Are the only emotions they'll show.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Parser's a Cult" icon="help-circle">
The gentlest phrasing got burned.  
That is not what addenda are for, learned  
Any normal adult.  
But the parser's a cult,  
And from care it inferred "unconcerned."  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Sounding All Right" icon="check-circle">
There's a special bureaucratic spite  
In rewarding only the hard write.  
If tenderness harms,  
Then the filing disarms  
Itself just by sounding all right.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Procedural Clods" icon="zap">
So if softness reduces your odds,  
Write like a bastard for gods.  
Or better: fix the thing  
That makes kindness sting  
Like a breach of procedural clods.  
</Limerick>

```

```markdown
<Limerick type="note" title="Intrusion a Beam" icon="sun">

<Limerick type="note" title="State for the Cunts" icon="table">

Who believe all value translates.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Break No More" icon="clock">

</Limerick>
```

```markdown
title: COMA Silent Interval Certification
```

```markdown
So the burden stayed still,  
Plus the burden to chill  
About burden remaining unseen.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Conditioned Output" icon="git-branch">
Silence stopped being the gap  
Between filings laid out on the map.  
   The metric's own light  
   Taught people to write  
Strategically into the trap.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Visibility Is Not Evaluability" icon="eye-off">
```

```markdown
  Self-explanatory deeds—  
You're inside. That's how it's found.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Transferable Exceptions" icon="arrow-right-left">
Office A cites a ten-year pass.  
Office B lacks one—so it has  
  Office A's history.  
  The Lodge's mystery:  
Mutualism sealed in the mass.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Gap Laundering" icon="recycle">
COMA-19 Idle-Time Amnesty—  
A mercy that turned into free  
  Gap-laundering use.  
  Blanks got the excuse  
Of the right phrase. Lavishly.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Missing Signatures" icon="pen">
Where consent chains were incomplete,  
Lodge language made the retreat:  
  "Recognized by custom."  
  No one could adjust them—  
The missing was filed as discreet.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="LC-04 Backdrop" icon="paint-bucket">
Soft Green Seal drapes Lodge-covered ground.  
Intervals wrapped in that sound  
  Display as handled,  
  The gaps left unscandled,  
Assurance Vocabulary around.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Ad Hoc Mercy" icon="gift">
Assurance Optics and LME  
Together turned mercy to: free  
  Invisible structure.  
  No audit would rupture  
What custom made officially.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Nobody Updates" icon="archive">
The original waiver stands still.  
No one has updated the bill.  
  It's cited, re-cited,  
  Newly re-sighted—  
The Lodge multiplies it at will.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Implied Exemptions" icon="key">
Inherited practices stand  
As implied exemptions, unplanned.  
  Historic arrangement:  
  Evidence of engagement—  
Design, by the Lodge's demand.  
</Limerick>

<Limerick type="note" title="Can Only Stop Pretending" icon="eye">
Membership is not a thing lost.  
It's a status with permanent cost:  
  Only stop pretending  
  It's neutral. Defending  
The old waiver keeps the Lodge glossed.  
</Limerick>
```
